  **Hardware/OS Context:**
  - OS: Ubuntu 20.04 (or similar Debian-based, x86_64)
  - Architecture: x86_64 (amd64)  
  - GPU: No NVIDIA GPU detected (Matrox G200eW3 only; NOT CUDA-capable)
  - Docker: Supported, but no GPU build features (BuildKit, Buildx OK)
  - Paths: Linux, deep directory structure (`/home/cc/EnvGym/data/...`)
  **Key Adjustments:**
  - Remove all CUDA/NVIDIA GPU instructions and dependencies.
  - Use only CPU-optimized builds of PyTorch and related packages.
  - Ensure `faiss-cpu` (NOT `faiss-gpu`), and avoid any CUDA toolkit/driver install.
  - Make sure all environment files, test cases, and instructions reflect CPU-only setup.
  - Paths and scripts should use Linux conventions.
  - Keep Python versions as specified; documentation builds remain on Python 3.11.
  - Storage and RAM: If large datasets or notebooks, recommend checking available disk and memory before running heavy jobs (not part of plan unless specified).
  - Docker/development tools: All instructions compatible with Ubuntu 20.04 and Docker; avoid Windows/macOS-specific steps unless cross-platform testing.

  **1. DOWNLOADS NEEDED:**
  - Anaconda (Python distribution):  
    [https://www.anaconda.com/products/distribution]  
    - Version: Python 3.9 (preferred), 3.10 (acceptable), 3.11 (required for docs build).
  - Python: 3.9 (main), 3.10 (acceptable), 3.11 (docs).
  - Kilosort package: Latest from PyPI (`kilosort[gui]`) or editable install from repo.
  - PyTorch (CPU version):  
    - Install `pytorch` from `pytorch` channel—**do NOT install `pytorch-cuda` or CUDA toolkit**.
    - Version: `torch>=1.6` required by Kilosort.
  - **DO NOT install CUDA toolkit or NVIDIA drivers.**
  - Jupyter Notebook (optional): `jupyter` or `notebook`.
  - Matplotlib (for plotting): `matplotlib`.
  - PyQt (GUI dependency):  
    - Options: `pyqt6`, `pyqt6.sip` (default), or `pyqt5`, `pyqt5.sip` if `PyQt5` detected.
    - Also: `pyqtgraph>=0.13.0`, `qtpy`.
    - Alternative backends: `PySide2`, `PySide6` supported.
  - NumPy: `numpy>=1.20.0`.
  - SciPy: `scipy`.

  - tqdm: `tqdm`.

    - PDF build support (e.g., `rst2pdf`, `latex` tools)

  1. Download/install Anaconda (Python 3.9 or 3.10 for main env; Python 3.11 for docs env if needed).

  4. Create new environment:
     - `conda create --name kilosort python=3.9`
     - Verify: `conda env list`.
  5. Activate environment:
     - `conda activate kilosort`

     - `pip install faiss-cpu`

       - `cd Kilosort`
       - `pip install -e .[gui]`
     - Verify: `python -c "import kilosort"`.

  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  # Install system dependencies

      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          wget \
          git \
          ca-certificates \
          build-essential \
          libglib2.0-0 \
          libxext6 \
          libsm6 \

          texlive-lang-all \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install Miniconda (Python 3.9)
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py39_24.3.0-0-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  # Copy environment.yml if present (for conda env build)
  COPY environment.yml /tmp/environment.yml
  # Create and activate conda environment
  RUN conda env update -n base -f /tmp/environment.yml && \
      conda clean -a -y
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /workspace
  # Ensure pip is up-to-date, install faiss-cpu in base env (if not from conda), and install kiloSort[gui] in editable mode if source present
  RUN pip install --upgrade pip && \
      if [ -f "setup.py" ]; then \
          pip install -e .[gui]; \
      fi
  # Install docs requirements if present
  RUN if [ -f "docs/requirements.txt" ]; then \
          pip install -r docs/requirements.txt; \
      fi
  # Set entrypoint to bash
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py39_24.3.0-0-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /workspace
  # Update pip and install requirements directly (no environment.yml present)
  RUN pip install --upgrade pip && \
      pip install -e .[gui]
  # Install docs requirements if present
  RUN if [ -f "docs/requirements.txt" ]; then \
          pip install -r docs/requirements.txt; \
      fi
  # Set entrypoint to bash
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

          wget \

          build-essential \

  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py39_24.3.0-0-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /workspace
  # Copy environment.yml if it exists and create conda environment
  COPY environment.yml /workspace/environment.yml
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda env create -f /workspace/environment.yml
  # Install editable package and extras using conda environment's pip
  RUN /opt/conda/envs/kilosort/bin/pip install --upgrade pip && \
      /opt/conda/envs/kilosort/bin/pip install -e .[gui]
  # Install docs requirements if present
  RUN if [ -f "docs/requirements.txt" ]; then \
          /opt/conda/envs/kilosort/bin/pip install -r docs/requirements.txt; \
      fi
  # Set entrypoint to bash at the repository root with environment activated
  WORKDIR /workspace
  ENTRYPOINT ["/opt/conda/bin/conda", "run", "-n", "kilosort", "/bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          wget \
          git \
          ca-certificates \
          build-essential \
          libglib2.0-0 \
          libxext6 \
          libsm6 \
          libxrender1 \
          libgl1-mesa-glx \
          libgl1 \
          xvfb \
          pandoc \
          latexmk \
          texlive-latex-recommended \
          texlive-latex-extra \
          texlive-fonts-recommended \
          texlive-fonts-extra \
          texlive-xetex \
          texlive-lang-all \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install Miniconda (Python 3.9)
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py39_24.3.0-0-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /workspace
  # Install editable package and extras using pip (since environment.yml is not present)
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/pip install --upgrade pip && \
      /opt/conda/bin/pip install -e .[gui]
  # Install docs requirements if present
  RUN if [ -f "docs/requirements.txt" ]; then \
          /opt/conda/bin/pip install -r docs/requirements.txt; \
      fi
  # Set entrypoint to bash at the repository root
  WORKDIR /workspace
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

NEXT:
  current progress
  - The Dockerfile is structured for Ubuntu 20.04 and installs all required system dependencies, including Miniconda (Python 3.9).
  - The repository is copied to `/workspace`, and either `environment.yml` or a manual `conda` environment is used to create the `kilosort` environment.
  - The build fails during the environment activation and package installation step: `RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate kilosort && pip install --upgrade pip && pip install -e .[gui] && if [ -f docs/requirements.txt ]; then pip install -r docs/requirements.txt; fi"` (exit code 1).
  - No CUDA/NVIDIA instructions are present; CPU-only setup is followed.
  - The failure occurs at activating the environment and running pip installs, indicating conda environment activation issues in Docker's non-interactive RUN context.
  next step
  - Replace the problematic environment activation and pip install step with the following pattern:
    ```
    RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install --upgrade pip
    RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install -e .[gui]
    RUN if [ -f docs/requirements.txt ]; then /opt/conda/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install -r docs/requirements.txt; fi
    ```
  - Remove the `/bin/bash -c "source ... && conda activate ..."` approach, as `conda activate` does not work reliably in Docker RUN commands.
  - Ensure `environment.yml` explicitly declares all required dependencies, including `pip` and `kilosort[gui]` under pip if not available via conda.
  - Rebuild the Docker image to confirm successful environment setup and package installation.

      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \

  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /workspace
  # Create environment from environment.yml if present
  RUN if [ -f "environment.yml" ]; then \
          /opt/conda/bin/conda env create -f environment.yml && \
          /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy; \
      else \
          /opt/conda/bin/conda create -y -n kilosort python=3.9 && \
          /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy; \
      fi
  # Activate environment and install editable package with gui extras
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda activate kilosort && \
      pip install --upgrade pip && \
      pip install -e .[gui] && \
      if [ -f docs/requirements.txt ]; then pip install -r docs/requirements.txt; fi"
  # Set entrypoint to bash at the repository root
  WORKDIR /workspace
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

    - Install `pytorch` from `pytorch` channel—**do NOT install `pytorch-cuda` or CUDA toolkit**.
    - Version: `torch>=1.6` required by Kilosort.
  - **DO NOT install CUDA toolkit or NVIDIA drivers.**
  - Jupyter Notebook (optional): `jupyter` or `notebook`.
  - Matplotlib (for plotting): `matplotlib`.
  - PyQt (GUI dependency):  
    - Options: `pyqt6`, `pyqt6.sip` (default), or `pyqt5`, `pyqt5.sip` if `PyQt5` detected.
    - Also: `pyqtgraph>=0.13.0`, `qtpy`.
    - Alternative backends: `PySide2`, `PySide6` supported.
  - NumPy: `numpy>=1.20.0`.
  - SciPy: `scipy`.
  - scikit-learn: `scikit-learn`.
  - tqdm: `tqdm`.
  - numba: `numba`.
  - faiss-cpu: `faiss-cpu` (**not faiss-gpu**).
  - Git (for cloning repo): [https://git-scm.com/downloads].

    - sphinx>=3.0
    - sphinxcontrib-apidoc
    - nbsphinx
    - myst_parser
    - sphinx_rtd_theme
    - pandoc
  - (Optional) Phy (in separate environment): [https://github.com/cortex-lab/phy]
  - Read the Docs requirements:
    - Python 3.11
    - Ubuntu 22.04
    - Sphinx config at `docs/conf.py`
    - PDF build support (e.g., `rst2pdf`, `latex` tools)
    - MkDocs (optional)
  - Version compatibility: Python 3.9/3.10 (main), 3.11 (docs), linux/macOS/windows testing.
  - All dependencies compatible with Sphinx, PyTorch (CPU), Kilosort, GUI libraries, notebook integration.

  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          wget \
          git \
          ca-certificates \
          build-essential \
          libglib2.0-0 \
          libxext6 \
          libsm6 \
          libxrender1 \
          libgl1-mesa-glx \
          libgl1 \
          xvfb \
          pandoc \
          latexmk \
          texlive-latex-recommended \
          texlive-latex-extra \
          texlive-fonts-recommended \
          texlive-fonts-extra \
          texlive-xetex \
          texlive-lang-all \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install Miniconda (Python 3.9)
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py39_24.3.0-0-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /workspace
  # Create environment from environment.yml if present
  RUN if [ -f "environment.yml" ]; then \
          /opt/conda/bin/conda env create -f environment.yml && \
          /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy; \
      else \
          /opt/conda/bin/conda create -y -n kilosort python=3.9 && \
          /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy; \
      fi
  # Install pip and packages using conda run
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install --upgrade pip
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install -e .[gui]
  RUN if [ -f docs/requirements.txt ]; then /opt/conda/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install -r docs/requirements.txt; fi
  # Set entrypoint to bash at the repository root
  WORKDIR /workspace
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          wget \
          git \
          ca-certificates \
          build-essential \
          libglib2.0-0 \
          libxext6 \
          libsm6 \
          libxrender1 \
          libgl1-mesa-glx \
          libgl1 \
          xvfb \
          pandoc \
          latexmk \
          texlive-latex-recommended \
          texlive-latex-extra \
          texlive-fonts-recommended \
          texlive-fonts-extra \
          texlive-xetex \
          texlive-lang-all \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install Miniconda (Python 3.9)
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py39_24.3.0-0-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /workspace
  # Create environment from environment.yml if present
  RUN if [ -f "environment.yml" ]; then \
          /opt/conda/bin/conda env create -f environment.yml && \
          /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy; \
      else \
          /opt/conda/bin/conda create -y -n kilosort python=3.9 && \
          /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy; \
      fi
  # Install GUI and build dependencies before editable install
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda install -n kilosort -y \
          pyqt \
          pyqtgraph \
          qtpy \
      && /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  # Upgrade pip and show environment state before install
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install --upgrade pip
  RUN ls -l /workspace && /opt/conda/bin/conda run -n kilosort conda list
  # Attempt editable install with [gui] extras; fallback to normal install if failure
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install -e .[gui] || /opt/conda/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install .[gui]
  # Install docs requirements if present
  RUN if [ -f docs/requirements.txt ]; then /opt/conda/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install -r docs/requirements.txt; fi
  # Set entrypoint to bash at the repository root
  WORKDIR /workspace
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]
